# I-arch-001f — e2e test with pinned AuditIR fixture (POST → graph → bundle → compare)

GH#468. Critical-path day 10. The capstone test that pins the I-arch-001a → I-arch-001e seam end-to-end so any future drift on run_store / actors / pipeline-A / bundle / stream / SSE-translation breaks one obvious assertion.

## Files I have ALSO checked clean (§-1.2 #2)

- `tests/polaris_v6/api/test_artifact_to_slice_chain.py` — has `_write_synthetic_artifact_dir(tmp_path, ...)` building a loader-valid AuditIR fixture with all 5 required JSON files (manifest, verification_details, bibliography, contradictions, report). Reusable.
- `tests/polaris_v6/api/test_bundle_endpoint_targz.py` (I-arch-001d) — already exercises the bundle endpoint with synthetic artifact + signer override + 404/422 paths. Has the pattern for `app.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn] = _stub_sign_fn`.
- `tests/v6/test_api_stream.py` (I-arch-001e) — has the fakeredis monkeypatch pattern for `stream_module.read_events`.
- `src/polaris_v6/api/app.py` — `create_app()` wires `/runs` + `/stream` + `/bundle` (need to confirm bundle router is included).
- `src/polaris_v6/api/runs.py:23-40` — POST /runs creates uuid → `run_store.insert_run` → `enqueue_research_run.send` → returns RunStatusResponse with lifecycle_status='queued'.
- `src/polaris_v6/queue/actors.py` — `enqueue_research_run.fn(run_id, payload)` is the Phase-0 stub returning `{"run_id": ..., "status": "completed", "echo": payload}` — does NOT call pipeline-A.
- `src/polaris_v6/queue/run_store.py` — `insert_run`, `mark_in_progress`, `set_pipeline_meta(query_slug, artifact_dir, manifest_run_id, decision_id)`, `mark_completed(run_id, result_json, pipeline_status, cost_usd)`, `get_run`.
- `src/polaris_v6/api/bundle.py` — `GET /runs/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz` reads run_store record, requires lifecycle_status='completed' + release_allowed=True, calls `build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)`, dispatches to `post_audit_bundle` with `Depends(get_sign_fn)`.
- `src/polaris_v6/queue/run_events.py` (I-arch-001e) — `emit_event` + `emit_terminal_event` + `read_events` + `translate`.

## Scope

Single test file `tests/v6/test_end_to_end_arch_001f.py` (~250 LOC) that hits:

1. **POST /runs** with `{template: "clinical", question: "..."}` → 202 + `RunStatusResponse(run_id=uuid, lifecycle_status="queued")`.
2. **Simulate pipeline-A side-effects** (the actor is a Phase-0 stub, so the test manually invokes the side-effects pipeline-A would produce):
   - `_write_synthetic_artifact_dir(tmp_path / run_id)` builds the AuditIR-shape directory.
   - `run_store.mark_in_progress(run_id)`.
   - `run_store.set_pipeline_meta(run_id, query_slug, artifact_dir, decision_id)`.
   - `run_events.emit_event(run_id, "scope_gate.completed", {...}, redis_client=sync_fake)` — stage event.
   - `run_events.emit_terminal_event(run_id, "success", redis_client=sync_fake)`.
   - `run_store.mark_completed(run_id, result_json, pipeline_status="success", cost_usd=0.42)`.
3. **GET /runs/{run_id}** → 200 + lifecycle_status="completed" + pipeline_status="success".
4. **GET /stream/{run_id}** → SSE response with `scope_decision` + `run_complete` v6 events (translated from pipeline-A naming via `run_events.translate`).
5. **GET /runs/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz** with `dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn] = _stub_sign_fn` → 200 application/gzip (or 503 gpg_unavailable if no override; assert NOT 503 with override).
6. **Compare assertions**: the bundle response carries `bundle_id` + a manifest with the same `run_id` UUID. The SSE stream's `run_complete.status` == manifest.status. The bundle's slice_chain.report.pipeline_verdict == "success".

## Acceptance criteria

1. Single hermetic e2e test using `fakeredis.FakeServer()` + `_write_synthetic_artifact_dir` (no real Redis, no real LLM, no real network).
2. Test passes against the polaris HEAD (post-I-arch-001e merge).
3. Test fails LOUDLY if any of:
   - `run_store.mark_completed` schema regression
   - `bundle.py` Depends() callable-identity regression (per I-arch-001d P1-001)
   - `stream.py` Last-Event-ID header semantics regression
   - `run_events.translate` mapping regression
   - `artifact_to_slice_chain` ScopeDecision / EvidencePool / VerifiedReport schema regression
4. Test runs in <5s wall-clock.
5. No mocking of `run_store` or `artifact_to_slice_chain` — those are exercised against the real implementations to catch real drift.

## Direct questions iter 1

1. Single e2e test (~250 LOC) covering 6 steps as the I-arch-001a-e capstone — APPROVE'd? Or want it split into 2 tests (one for POST→stream, one for POST→bundle)?
2. Synthetic AuditIR fixture reused from `tests/polaris_v6/api/test_artifact_to_slice_chain.py::_write_synthetic_artifact_dir` rather than promoted to a shared conftest — APPROVE'd, or want it promoted in this same PR?
3. fakeredis-backed SSE rather than real-Redis integration test — APPROVE'd for I-arch-001f (hermetic CI bar), with real-Redis e2e captured as a separate post-deploy smoke test?
4. Test file path `tests/v6/test_end_to_end_arch_001f.py` — APPROVE'd? Or prefer `tests/v6/test_e2e_pipeline_a_seam.py`?
5. Anything else blocking iter-1 APPROVE?

 230: def get_run(run_id: str, *, path: str | None = None) -> RunStatusResponse | None:
 231:     """Return the run record or None if missing.
 232: 
 233:     Defensive against `OperationalError: no such table` so callers in stub
 234:     mode (e.g. `tests/v6/test_actors.py` direct `.fn()` invocation without
 235:     init_db) get None back, matching the actor's row-missing-stub-noop
 236:     contract.
 237: 
 238:     I-arch-001a Codex iter-2 P2-002: if a known DB exists with the legacy
 239:     schema, the first read-only `get_run` call would 500 on column-missing.
 240:     The defensive catch below detects "no such column" and triggers a
 241:     one-time migration via init_db before retrying.
 242:     """
 243:     conn = _connect(path)
 244:     try:
 245:         try:
 246:             row = conn.execute(
 247:                 "SELECT run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
 248:                 "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
 249:                 "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id "
 250:                 "FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 251:                 (run_id,),
 252:             ).fetchone()
 253:         except sqlite3.OperationalError as exc:
 254:             msg = str(exc).lower()
 255:             # Narrow per Codex iter-1 P2-001: only the missing-table stub
 256:             # path returns None; surface other operational errors (schema
 257:             # corruption, migration faults) so they aren't masked as
 258:             # missing-row.
 259:             if "no such table" in msg:
 260:                 return None
 261:             # Codex iter-2 P2-002: legacy schema → migrate then retry once.
 262:             if "no such column" in msg:
 263:                 conn.close()
 264:                 init_db(path)
 265:                 conn = _connect(path)
 266:                 row = conn.execute(
 267:                     "SELECT run_id, template, question, lifecycle_status, pipeline_status, "
 268:                     "queued_at, started_at, finished_at, result_json, error_json, "
 269:                     "query_slug, manifest_run_id, artifact_dir, cost_usd, decision_id "
 270:                     "FROM runs WHERE run_id=?",
 271:                     (run_id,),
 272:                 ).fetchone()
 273:             else:
 274:                 raise
 275:     finally:
 276:         conn.close()
 277:     if row is None:
 278:         return None
 279:     return RunStatusResponse(
 280:         run_id=row["run_id"],
 281:         template=row["template"],
 282:         question=row["question"],
 283:         lifecycle_status=row["lifecycle_status"],
 284:         pipeline_status=row["pipeline_status"],
 285:         queued_at=row["queued_at"],
 286:         started_at=row["started_at"],

 succeeded in 1132ms:
  68: @router.get("/{run_id}/bundle.tar.gz")
  69: def get_run_bundle_targz(
  70:     run_id: str,
  71:     sign_fn=Depends(get_sign_fn),
  72: ):
  73:     """Resolve run_id → artifact_dir → signed audit bundle (tar.gz).
  74: 
  75:     I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-1 P1-001: `Depends(get_sign_fn)` MUST use
  76:     the actual `get_sign_fn` callable from audit_bundle_route — the
  77:     create_app() registers `app.dependency_overrides[get_sign_fn]` to
  78:     inject the real GPGSigner when POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set. A lambda
  79:     Depends would be a different callable; the override would never fire.
  80: 
  81:     Status codes:
  82:         200: bundleable run; returns application/gzip
  83:         404: run not found, not completed, or artifact_dir missing
  84:         422: run aborted (pipeline_status=abort_*) or sovereignty cascade
  85:              emptied the report
  86:         503: GPG signer not configured (POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID unset) — surfaced
  87:              by the inner post_audit_bundle when sign_fn is None.
  88:     """
  89:     info = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  90:     if info is None:
  91:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail={"error": "run not found"})
  92:     if info.lifecycle_status != "completed":
  93:         raise HTTPException(
  94:             status_code=404,
  95:             detail={"error": f"run not completed: lifecycle_status={info.lifecycle_status}"},
  96:         )
  97:     if info.pipeline_status and info.pipeline_status.startswith("abort_"):
  98:         raise HTTPException(
  99:             status_code=422,
 100:             detail={"error": f"run aborted: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status}", "bundleable": False},
 101:         )
 102:     if not info.artifact_dir:
 103:         raise HTTPException(
 104:             status_code=404, detail={"error": "run has no artifact_dir recorded"}
 105:         )
 106: 
 107:     artifact_dir = Path(info.artifact_dir)
 108:     if not artifact_dir.is_dir():
 109:         raise HTTPException(
 110:             status_code=404,
 111:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir does not exist on disk: {artifact_dir}"},
 112:         )
 113: 
 114:     # I-arch-001d Codex diff iter-2 P1-002 fix: release_allowed gate.
 115:     # The slice-chain pipeline_verdict collapses partial_* into "success",
 116:     # but a release-blocked partial (e.g. partial_qwen_advisory with
 117:     # release_allowed=false) MUST NOT ship as a clean bundle. Read the raw
 118:     # manifest.release_allowed flag and refuse with 422 when False.
 119:     try:
 120:         manifest_raw = json.loads((artifact_dir / "manifest.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 121:     except (OSError, json.JSONDecodeError) as exc:
 122:         raise HTTPException(
 123:             status_code=404,
 124:             detail={"error": f"manifest.json missing or invalid: {exc}"},
 125:         ) from exc
 126:     if not manifest_raw.get("release_allowed", False):
 127:         raise HTTPException(
 128:             status_code=422,
 129:             detail={
 130:                 "error": (
 131:                     f"run release-blocked: pipeline_status={info.pipeline_status!r}, "
 132:                     f"release_allowed=False. Bundle cannot ship until release gate clears."
 133:                 ),
 134:                 "bundleable": False,
 135:                 "pipeline_status": info.pipeline_status,
 136:             },
 137:         )
 138: 
 139:     try:
 140:         decision, pool, report = build_slice_chain(artifact_dir)
 141:     except SovereigntyFilterEmptiedReportError as exc:
 142:         raise HTTPException(status_code=422, detail={"error": str(exc)}) from exc
 143:     except FileNotFoundError as exc:
 144:         raise HTTPException(
 145:             status_code=404,
 146:             detail={"error": f"artifact_dir incomplete: {exc}"},
 147:         ) from exc
 148: 
 149:     return post_audit_bundle(
 150:         AuditBundleRequest(decision=decision, pool=pool, report=report),
 151:         sign_fn=sign_fn,
 152:     )

   1: """SSE /stream endpoint — durable replayable event log via Redis Streams.
   2: 
   3: I-arch-001e (2026-05-13): replaces canned Phase 0 demo events with real
   4: Redis-Streams-backed SSE. Honors Last-Event-ID HTTP header (set
   5: automatically by EventSource on reconnect) plus ?last_event_id= query
   6: param fallback. Emits each event with `id: <stream_id>` so EventSource
   7: clients resume cleanly. Terminates after a v6 `run_complete` event.
   8: 
   9: Per docs/carney_delivery_plan_v6_2.md F4, the v6 event protocol is:
  10: scope_decision, retrieval_progress, evidence_id, verifier_verdict,
  11: section_complete, run_complete. Pipeline-A's stage events translate to
  12: these names via polaris_v6.queue.run_events.translate().
  13: """
  14: 
  15: from __future__ import annotations
  16: 
  17: import json
  18: from typing import AsyncIterator
  19: 
  20: from fastapi import APIRouter, Header
  21: from sse_starlette.sse import EventSourceResponse
  22: 
  23: from polaris_v6.queue.run_events import read_events, translate
  24: 
  25: router = APIRouter(prefix="/stream", tags=["stream"])
  26: 
  27: 
  28: async def _redis_stream_source(
  29:     run_id: str, last_event_id: str, *, redis_client_async=None
  30: ) -> AsyncIterator[dict]:
  31:     """Yield SSE event dicts sourced from the Redis Stream for this run_id.
  32: 
  33:     Each yielded event includes `id: <stream_id>` so the EventSource client
  34:     resumes via Last-Event-ID on reconnect. Empty XREAD windows yield a
  35:     keepalive comment frame. Terminates after a v6 `run_complete`.
  36:     """
  37:     async for stream_id, raw_event in read_events(
  38:         run_id,
  39:         last_event_id=last_event_id,
  40:         redis_client_async=redis_client_async,
  41:     ):
  42:         if stream_id == "__keepalive__":
  43:             yield {"comment": "keepalive"}
  44:             continue
  45:         v6 = translate(raw_event)
  46:         if v6 is None:
  47:             continue
  48:         v6_name, v6_payload = v6
  49:         yield {
  50:             "id": stream_id,
  51:             "event": v6_name,
  52:             "data": json.dumps({"run_id": run_id, **v6_payload}),
  53:         }
  54:         if v6_name == "run_complete":
  55:             return
  56: 
  57: 
  58: @router.get("/{run_id}")
  59: async def stream_run(
  60:     run_id: str,
  61:     last_event_id_header: str | None = Header(None, alias="Last-Event-ID"),
  62:     last_event_id: str = "0-0",
  63: ) -> EventSourceResponse:
  64:     """SSE event stream for a research run.
  65: 
  66:     Reconnect / replay semantics:
  67:         - HTTP `Last-Event-ID: <stream_id>` header (set automatically by
  68:           EventSource on reconnect)
  69:         - `?last_event_id=<stream_id>` query param fallback for manual clients
  70:     """
  71:     effective = last_event_id_header or last_event_id
  72:     return EventSourceResponse(_redis_stream_source(run_id, effective))

 150:     app_with_bundle_router, isolated_db, tmp_path
 151: ):
 152:     """When a sign_fn override IS registered, build_slice_chain runs and the
 153:     bundle returns 200 with application/gzip. This is the key P1-001 regression:

 161:         "run_signed",

 167:         "run_signed",
 168:         {"manifest": {"status": "success"}, "status": "success"},

 171:         path=str(isolated_db),
 172:     )

 174:     # Install a stub signer override (returns synthetic signature bytes).
 175:     def _stub_sign_fn():

 177:             return b"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\nstub\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n"
 178:         return _sign

  48: 
  49: def _parse_sse(raw: str) -> list[dict]:
  50:     """Parse the SSE wire format into a list of {event, data, id} dicts.
  51: 
  52:     Tolerates the keepalive comment (`: keepalive\\n\\n`) by skipping blocks
  53:     that contain no `event:` line.
  54:     """
  55:     normalized = raw.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
  56:     events: list[dict] = []
  57:     for block in normalized.split("\n\n"):
  58:         block = block.strip()
  59:         if not block:
  60:             continue
  61:         evt: dict = {}
  62:         for line in block.splitlines():
  63:             line = line.strip()
  64:             if line.startswith(":"):
  65:                 # comment / keepalive
  66:                 continue
  67:             if line.startswith("event:"):
  68:                 evt["event"] = line[len("event:"):].strip()
  69:             elif line.startswith("data:"):
  70:                 evt["data"] = json.loads(line[len("data:"):].strip())
  71:             elif line.startswith("id:"):
  72:                 evt["id"] = line[len("id:"):].strip()
  73:         if evt.get("event"):
  74:             events.append(evt)
  75:     return events
  76:

   2: 
   3: I-phase0-005 (Codex APPROVE iter 4): persist runs to SQLite via
   4: polaris_v6.queue.run_store and enqueue the Dramatiq actor on POST.
   5: Replaces the previous in-memory `_run_table` dict.
   6: """
   7: 
   8: from __future__ import annotations
   9: 
  10: import sqlite3
  11: import uuid
  12: 
  13: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
  14: 
  15: from polaris_v6.queue import run_store
  16: from polaris_v6.queue.actors import enqueue_research_run
  17: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_request import RunRequest
  18: from polaris_v6.schemas.run_status import RunStatusResponse
  19: 
  20: router = APIRouter(prefix="/runs", tags=["runs"])
  21: 
  22: 
  23: @router.post("", response_model=RunStatusResponse, status_code=202)
  24: def create_run(payload: RunRequest) -> RunStatusResponse:
  25:     run_id = uuid.uuid4().hex
  26:     try:
  27:         run_store.insert_run(run_id, payload.template, payload.question)
  28:     except sqlite3.IntegrityError as exc:
  29:         # uuid4 collision is theoretically impossible but defensive
  30:         raise HTTPException(status_code=409, detail=f"run {run_id!r} already exists") from exc
  31:     except RuntimeError as exc:
  32:         # init_db permission-denied or similar
  33:         raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail=str(exc)) from exc
  34: 
  35:     enqueue_research_run.send(run_id, payload.model_dump())
  36: 
  37:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  38:     if record is None:  # pragma: no cover — insert just succeeded
  39:         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="run row vanished after insert")
  40:     return record
  41: 
  42: 
  43: @router.get("/{run_id}", response_model=RunStatusResponse)
  44: def get_run(run_id: str) -> RunStatusResponse:
  45:     record = run_store.get_run(run_id)
  46:     if record is None:
  47:         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"run {run_id!r} not found")
  48:     return record

 127: def build_manifest_and_files(
 128:     decision: ScopeDecision,
 129:     pool: EvidencePool,
 130:     report: VerifiedReport,
 131: ) -> tuple[BundleManifest, dict[str, bytes]]:
 132:     """Build the bundle manifest + content-file dict.
 133: 
 134:     Returns:
 135:         (manifest, files) where files is {path: content_bytes}. The
 136:         caller (bundle_builder) packs files into a tarball and writes
 137:         the manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc alongside.
 138: 
 139:     Raises:
 140:         ValueError if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success'.
 141:     """
 142:     if report.pipeline_verdict != "success":
 143:         raise ValueError(
 144:             f"cannot build audit bundle for verdict "
 145:             f"{report.pipeline_verdict!r}; report must be successful"
 146:         )
 147: 
 148:     files_bytes: dict[str, bytes] = {}
 149: 
 150:     # 1. Slice 001 ScopeDecision
 151:     sd_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(decision)
 152:     files_bytes[FILE_SCOPE_DECISION] = sd_bytes
 153: 
 154:     # 2. Slice 002 EvidencePool
 155:     ep_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(pool)
 156:     files_bytes[FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL] = ep_bytes
 157: 
 158:     # 3. Slice 003 VerifiedReport
 159:     vr_bytes = _serialize_json_canonical(report)
 160:     files_bytes[FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT] = vr_bytes
 161: 
 162:     # 4. Sovereignty: refuse to ship verbatim spans for non-cleared sources
 163:     assert_all_pool_sources_legal_cleared(pool)
 164: 
 165:     # 4b. Per-source snapshots + cited-span reachability guard
 166:     snapshot_entries = snapshot_sources_with_reachable(report, pool)
 167:     _assert_cited_spans_reachable(report, snapshot_entries)
 168:     for source_id, entry in snapshot_entries.items():
 169:         files_bytes[_safe_source_filename(source_id)] = entry.text.encode("utf-8")
 170:     snapshots = {sid: e.text for sid, e in snapshot_entries.items()}
 171: 
 172:     # 4b. REVIEWER_README ships verbatim in every bundle as metadata content_type.
 173:     readme_path = Path(__file__).parent / "REVIEWER_README.md"
 174:     files_bytes[FILE_REVIEWER_README] = readme_path.read_bytes()
 175: 
 176:     # 5. Bundle metadata (versions + creation timestamp)
 177:     metadata = {
 178:         "bundle_version": BUNDLE_VERSION,
 179:         "polaris_version": POLARIS_VERSION,
 180:         "created_at_utc": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat().replace(
 181:             "+00:00", "Z"
 182:         ),
 183:         "generator_model": report.generator_model,
 184:         "decision_id": decision.decision_id,
 185:         "pool_id": report.pool_id,
 186:         "report_id": report.report_id,
 187:         "source_snapshot_count": len(snapshots),
 188:     }
 189:     files_bytes[FILE_METADATA] = json.dumps(
 190:         metadata,
 191:         sort_keys=True,
 192:         ensure_ascii=False,
 193:         separators=(",", ":"),
 194:     ).encode("utf-8")
 195: 
 196:     # Build FileEntry list with content_type tags
 197:     file_entries: list[FileEntry] = []
 198:     content_type_by_path = {
 199:         FILE_SCOPE_DECISION: "scope_decision",
 200:         FILE_EVIDENCE_POOL: "evidence_pool",
 201:         FILE_VERIFIED_REPORT: "verified_report",
 202:         FILE_METADATA: "metadata",
 203:     }
 204:     for path, content in files_bytes.items():
 205:         ct = content_type_by_path.get(
 206:             path,
 207:             "source_snapshot" if path.startswith(SOURCES_DIR + "/") else "metadata",
 208:         )
 209:         file_entries.append(
 210:             FileEntry(
 211:                 path=path,
 212:                 sha256=_sha256_bytes(content),
 213:                 size_bytes=len(content),
 214:                 content_type=ct,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
 215:             )
 216:         )
 217: 
 218:     # Sort entries deterministically for stable manifest output
 219:     file_entries.sort(key=lambda f: f.path)
 220: 
 221:     manifest = BundleManifest(
 222:         decision_id=decision.decision_id,
 223:         pool_id=report.pool_id,
 224:         report_id=report.report_id,
 225:         generator_model=report.generator_model,
 226:         polaris_version=POLARIS_VERSION,
 227:         files=file_entries,
 228:     )
 229:     return manifest, files_bytes
 230: 
 231: 
 232: def serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest: BundleManifest) -> bytes:
 233:     """Produce canonical YAML bytes for GPG signing.
 234: 
 235:     PyYAML default_flow_style=False + sort_keys=True keeps it stable
 236:     across re-serializations.
 237:     """
 238:     payload = manifest.model_dump(mode="json")
 239:     return yaml.safe_dump(
 240:         payload,
 241:         default_flow_style=False,
 242:         sort_keys=True,
 243:         allow_unicode=True,
 244:     ).encode("utf-8")

  90: @router.post("/audit-bundle")
  91: def post_audit_bundle(
  92:     req: AuditBundleRequest,
  93:     sign_fn: SignFn | None = Depends(get_sign_fn),
  94: ) -> Any:
  95:     """Build + return a GPG-signed audit bundle as application/gzip.
  96: 
  97:     Returns the .tar.gz file as a streaming download.
  98:     """
  99:     if sign_fn is None:
 100:         raise HTTPException(
 101:             status_code=503,
 102:             detail={
 103:                 "error": True,
 104:                 "code": "gpg_unavailable",
 105:                 "message": (
 106:                     "GPG signer not configured. Set POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID in env "
 107:                     "and ensure the corresponding key is in the gpg keyring."
 108:                 ),
 109:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 110:             },
 111:         )
 112: 
 113:     # Build into a temp dir; FileResponse copies it to the wire.
 114:     tmp_dir = Path(tempfile.mkdtemp(prefix="polaris_audit_"))
 115:     try:
 116:         bundle_path = build_audit_bundle(
 117:             req.decision,
 118:             req.pool,
 119:             req.report,
 120:             output_dir=tmp_dir,
 121:             sign_fn=sign_fn,
 122:         )
 123:     except ValueError as exc:
 124:         # FK chain mismatch, verdict != success, cited-span unreachable, or copyrighted span
 125:         msg = str(exc)
 126:         if "copyrighted span" in msg:
 127:             code = "copyrighted_span_in_bundle"
 128:         elif "cited span unreachable" in msg:
 129:             code = "cited_span_unreachable_after_snapshot"
 130:         elif "FK chain" in msg or "pool_id" in msg or "decision_id" in msg:
 131:             code = "fk_chain_mismatch"
 132:         else:
 133:             code = "verdict_not_success"
 134:         raise HTTPException(
 135:             status_code=400,
 136:             detail={
 137:                 "error": True,
 138:                 "code": code,
 139:                 "message": msg,
 140:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 141:             },
 142:         )
 143:     except RuntimeError as exc:
 144:         raise HTTPException(
 145:             status_code=502,
 146:             detail={
 147:                 "error": True,
 148:                 "code": "sign_failed",
 149:                 "message": str(exc),
 150:                 "report_id": req.report.report_id,
 151:             },
 152:         )
 153: 
 154:     return FileResponse(
 155:         path=str(bundle_path),
 156:         filename=bundle_path.name,
 157:         media_type="application/gzip",
 158:     )

  80:     """End-to-end: build manifest + sign + pack tarball.
  81: 
  82:     Args:
  83:         decision: slice 001 ScopeDecision
  84:         pool: slice 002 EvidencePool (must match report.pool_id)
  85:         report: slice 003 VerifiedReport (must have verdict=success)
  86:         output_dir: directory where audit_<id>.tar.gz is written
  87:         sign_fn: function that takes manifest.yaml bytes and returns
  88:                  .asc bytes. Default raises NotImplementedError; callers
  89:                  MUST inject a real signer.
  90: 
  91:     Returns:
  92:         Path to the generated audit_<bundle_id>.tar.gz file.
  93: 
  94:     Raises:
  95:         ValueError: if report.pipeline_verdict != 'success' or pool/report
  96:                     FK chain inconsistent.
  97:         RuntimeError: if sign_fn raises (propagated, original error chained).
  98:     """
  99:     if report.pool_id != pool.pool_id:
 100:         raise ValueError(
 101:             f"FK chain mismatch: report.pool_id={report.pool_id!r} != "
 102:             f"pool.pool_id={pool.pool_id!r}"
 103:         )
 104:     if report.decision_id != decision.decision_id:
 105:         raise ValueError(
 106:             f"FK chain mismatch: report.decision_id={report.decision_id!r}"
 107:             f" != decision.decision_id={decision.decision_id!r}"
 108:         )
 109: 
 110:     t_start = time.perf_counter()
 111:     manifest, content_files = build_manifest_and_files(decision, pool, report)
 112: 
 113:     manifest_yaml = serialize_manifest_yaml(manifest)
 114: 
 115:     try:
 116:         manifest_sig = sign_fn(manifest_yaml)
 117:     except NotImplementedError:
 118:         raise RuntimeError(
 119:             "audit bundle requires a sign_fn; default sentinel forbids "
 120:             "shipping unsigned bundles per CLAUDE.md LAW II"
 121:         )
 122:     except Exception as exc:
 123:         raise RuntimeError(
 124:             f"sign_fn raised {type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
 125:         ) from exc
 126: 
 127:     # Pack everything into a single .tar.gz under top-level dir audit_<id>
 128:     output_dir = Path(output_dir)
 129:     output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 130:     bundle_filename = f"audit_{manifest.bundle_id}.tar.gz"
 131:     bundle_path = output_dir / bundle_filename
 132: 
 133:     with tarfile.open(bundle_path, "w:gz") as tar:
 134:         top_dir = f"audit_{manifest.bundle_id}"
 135: 
 136:         # 1. manifest.yaml + manifest.yaml.asc (NOT in manifest.files;
 137:         #    they are the manifest itself + signature)
 138:         _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/manifest.yaml", manifest_yaml)
 139:         _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/manifest.yaml.asc", manifest_sig)
 140: 
 141:         # 2. Content files (paths from manifest.files)
 142:         for path, content_bytes in content_files.items():
 143:             _add_file(tar, f"{top_dir}/{path}", content_bytes)
 144: 
 145:     elapsed_ms = int((time.perf_counter() - t_start) * 1000)
 146:     _LOG.info(
 147:         "audit bundle built bundle_id=%s files=%d size=%dB elapsed=%dms",
 148:         manifest.bundle_id,
 149:         len(manifest.files),
 150:         bundle_path.stat().st_size,
 151:         elapsed_ms,
 152:     )
 153:     return bundle_path

 156: def _add_file(tar: tarfile.TarFile, name: str, data: bytes) -> None:
 157:     """Add bytes to a tarfile under `name`."""
 158:     info = tarfile.TarInfo(name=name)
 159:     info.size = len(data)
 160:     info.mtime = int(time.time())

  36: 
  37: 
  38: def _connect(path: str | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
  39:     resolved = _resolve_path(path)
  40:     parent = os.path.dirname(resolved)
  41:     if parent:
  42:         os.makedirs(parent, exist_ok=True)
  43:     conn = sqlite3.connect(resolved)
  44:     conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
  45:     return conn
  46: 
  47: 
  48: def _migrate_schema(conn: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
  49:     """Idempotent additive migration. Safe to call on every init_db.
  50: 
  51:     1. Create base table if absent.
  52:     2. If legacy `status` column exists and `lifecycle_status` doesn't,
  53:        RENAME COLUMN to preserve values (SQLite 3.25+, Python 3.11 ships
  54:        SQLite 3.34+).
  55:     3. ADD COLUMN for each I-arch-001a field if missing.
  56:     4. CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS for query lookups.
  57:     """
  58:     conn.execute(
  59:         """
  60:         CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS runs (
  61:             run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  62:             template TEXT NOT NULL,
  63:             question TEXT NOT NULL,
  64:             lifecycle_status TEXT NOT NULL,
  65:             queued_at TEXT NOT NULL,
  66:             started_at TEXT,
  67:             finished_at TEXT,
  68:             result_json TEXT,
  69:             error_json TEXT
  70:         )
  71:         """
  72:     )
  73:     cols = {row[1] for row in conn.execute("PRAGMA table_info(runs)").fetchall()}
  74:     if "status" in cols and "lifecycle_status" not in cols:
  75:         conn.execute("ALTER TABLE runs RENAME COLUMN status TO lifecycle_status")
  76:         cols.discard("status")
  77:         cols.add("lifecycle_status")
  78:     for col_name, col_type in {
  79:         "query_slug": "TEXT",
  80:         "manifest_run_id": "TEXT",
  81:         "artifact_dir": "TEXT",
  82:         "pipeline_status": "TEXT",
  83:         "cost_usd": "REAL",
  84:         "decision_id": "TEXT",
  85:     }.items():
  86:         if col_name not in cols:
  87:             conn.execute(f"ALTER TABLE runs ADD COLUMN {col_name} {col_type}")
  88:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_query_slug ON runs(query_slug)")
  89:     conn.execute("CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_runs_manifest_run_id ON runs(manifest_run_id)")
  90: 
  91: 
  92: def init_db(path: str | None = None) -> None:
  93:     """Create the runs table if absent, run migrations. Idempotent."""
  94:     conn = _connect(path)
  95:     try:

  56: def _derive_slug(template_id: str, question: str) -> str:
  57:     """Deterministic URL-safe slug for pipeline-A run_dir nesting.
  58: 
  59:     Pipeline-A reads q['slug']; this produces a stable, human-readable
  60:     identifier per (template, question) pair. UUID provides uniqueness
  61:     via the artifact_dir parent — slug itself doesn't need to be unique.
  62:     """
  63:     base = f"{template_id}_{question[:60]}"
  64:     cleaned = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9_]+", "_", base.lower()).strip("_")
  65:     return cleaned[:120] or "untitled"

  69: def enqueue_research_run(run_id: str, request_payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
  70:     """Execute a research run via pipeline-A. Idempotent on run_id.
  71:

  73:     .fn() directly without insert_run), returns deterministic noop
  74:     without DB writes — preserves I-phase0-005 stub-mode semantics.

  76:     Production path: marks in_progress, builds q-dict with v6 fields,

  92:     question = request_payload.get("question", "")

 215:     # ─── 1. ScopeDecision ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

 235:     )
